<Rate>4</Rate><Text>Went in to shop as opposed to pawn. Offered assistance only after we were leaving. Nice store, great range of products, and pretty organized. For tools, items were mostly medium to heavy wear, and thus the asking price seemed a bit high. Jewelry was in excellent condition and displayed beautifully. Poor price if evaluating based on scrap value plus item condition but a great price for people wanting something quick, specific, and competitively priced compared to chain stores. Would definitely recommend checking out. I think there's almost always something for most people in pawn stores, and this was one of the nicer stores in the area.

< date>
1488401388183<//date>
<Rate>4<//Rate>< Review>
What's not to love? Clarks, well made shoes that feel good  when you put them on. And bonus, if you are me they will always have size 11s on hand. Usually. My main reason for marking it down to a 4 is the price. I bought a pair of tennis shoes that I desperately needed and could not find in the color and size online from their site. I was thrilled. There was a sign on the door that said, Buy One Get One 50% off. Great. While I'm there, since attractive, comfortable, well fitting shoes are hard for me, I got a second pair. Only wouldn't you know it. The BOGO did not apply to my two selections. And more frustrating, the salesman came out and said the one pair was no longer being made and that these particular style had been returned to the main site. Somehow this pair got missed. (Which explains why I couldn't find them online, ha ha) seems to me if the style is getting "tired" and old, it should be reduced. Nope 140.00. Rape for comfort. Was it worth it? Probably. If you wear average sized shoes and like to save money. I would never recommend Clark's. But if you are like me and are tired of your feet hurting, get a second job to pay for these wonderful shoes because Clark's is not in the habit of having any decent sales on the better styles, or if they do you can bet the odd sizes no longer exist...< /Review>

<time>1558993482218< /time><rating>3</rating>< text>
The food was delicious and everything that we ordered was cooked perfectly. It was on the pricier side for dining in Ukiah. The service was incredibly slow and our dinner for two took more than 2 hours to get through. Our waitress checked on us only once during the meal and our water glasses remained empty for most of the main course. We also ordered drinks that were never delivered, and of course they attempted to charge us for them when the bill came due.

Overall, the experience was poor and the only saving grace was the excellent food.</text>

<UserId.>104391725146946372378</UserId.>< username>
Julie Healon<//username>
<date>1542042945740<//date>< Rating>
4<//Rating>
< Text>
We were staying at The Hampton Inn next door. We figured we can easily walk over, so made reservations. We called, and left a message, and it says they will call you backin a half hour. Nobody ever did. So, we booked online.

Very nice inside. Set up is a bit odd. When you walk in, there are tables, and a guy playing a piano. The host stand is down a bit. Odd. They are usually at the door.

We were 15 minutes early, so we had to wait a few minutes. While waiting, some old guy (owner or manager?) came and shoved some papers in one of the Hostess face, yelling at her to redo this, it's all wrong. No idea what it was. But she was clearly embarrassed. He needs to learn how to treat people, and not do something like that in front of her customers and co workers. Very rude!

None of the drinks sounded great, so we got sodas. They bring bread with vinegar and oil. So good!  The bread is like soft clouds. Not enough oil and vinegar though. We asked for more.

We got the fried ravioli for an appetizer. They were good. We didn't really care for the breading too much, but still enjoyed them. Came with marinara for dipping.

I got the ribs. They were super tender. The bbq sauce was super sweet. A little too sweet for my taste. But good. The poppy seed slaw was ok. Very few poppy seeds, and not a lot of flavor. Garlic fries were good. Regular fries with a glob of garlic on top. Could be done better.

Hubby got the two lobster tails with a baked potato. He said it's the best lobster he's had in awhile. They forgot butter, so we had to ask. He asked for lemon, which he never got. They are skimpy on the potato toppings.

We also got the brussel sprouts with bacon. They were really good. A bit hard. Could be cooked longer. We took dessert to go. The butterscotch bread pudding which was so good! Yum! And the chocolate lava cake. Also super yummy.

The atmosphere was nice. Our server was nice. No smiles. She seemed stressed or overworked. Definitely tired. It's clear that management is poor here.<//Text>

< Review>
The restaurant is very nice.  The food is very good and during happy hour less expensive in the bar on that menu.  The samplings are generous and not all of the menu from the restaurant is available for special pricing.  The most popular items , however are worth the happy hour savings. A piano player with the music from a small grand piano will welcome you in a small Fourier.  It is very nice and the entrance opens to a beautiful restuarant.  The service in the restaurant is much better than the bar.  However, the atmosphere in one aspect may be more gentle, the bar has a fair sophistication that should warrant better service than given.  Don't lose sight of it , it is a nice bar.  Also a very nice addition to be able to walk from the Hampton outside along the pool to the gate of the restaurant parking lot.  It is a nice recommendation and one you will be glad you tried.  The holiday meals are definitely worth the reservation.</Review>

< review>
Had an excellent dinner tonight with three friends at Crush.  Our server, Dawn was both cordial and professional.  She paced our meal perfectly so just as we were finishing the appetizer and salads, she and another staff delivered four freshly prepared plates of delicious jumbo shrimp scampi,  chicken alfredo, chicken picata, and chicken parmesan.  Each was expertly plated and piping hot from the kitchen.
The wine list is ample and offered various vintages from local wineries as well as some from other locales.
We usually just hit the pub for dark beer and  fish & chips, but I highly recommend sitting down for a full meal to appreciate the real quality available at this location.</review>

More than half the steak was fat, and her six prawns were also Burt and tough.  Definitely not worth $50 it cost.  I had the New York and a lobster tail, with truffle fries, and the house Clam Chowder.  My steak which I ordered Med. Rare, was half rare, and half medium. I used to have great food at Crush, but it seems that the "Ukiah curse" has taken this place over.
